innovations on this mega-ship has been inspired by some engineering greats. \\r\\n\\r\\nThis show will feature the work of Alvin Lombard, whose breakthrough continuous tracked logging machine, created in the early 1900s, changed the industrial world; Wilhelm Albert, whose wire rope revolutionized the 19th century mining; and Henry Kaiser, whose pioneering ship building techniques in 1940s America Designed to enlarge the existing 100-year-old canal, this $5.25 billion dollar project has redefined world trade routes. By excavating 150 million cubic tons of earth, and by pouring over 4 million cubic meters of concrete, engineers have created two brand-new gigantic flights of locks. Each lock is the length of four football fields, and is controlled by 1650,000 ton steel gates, which enables an unparalleled lift of 26 meters above sea level. inside the ambitious engineering project that remade the famous Panama Canal. Billions of dollars were spent to move millions of cubic tons of earth, and ultimately, the canal will be able to accommodate the biggest ships in the world.&quot;,&quot;detailed&quot;:&quot;Opened in 2016, the Panama Canal Extension is an engineering project of unprecedented scale. Designed to enlarge the existing 100-year-old canal, this $5.25 billion dollar project has redefined world trade routes. By excavating 150 million cubic tons of earth, and by pouring over 4 million cubic meters of concrete, engineers have created two brand-new gigantic flights of locks. Each lock is the length of four football fields, and is controlled by 1650,000 ton steel gates, which enables an unparalleled lift of 26 meters above sea level. The canal is now capable of accommodating the biggest ships on the world's oceans.\\r\\n\\r\\nNone of this would be possible without the work of history's greatest innovators. We feature the engineering greats responsible for the achievement of the Panama Canal Extension: 17th century engineer Hugues Cosnier, who revolutionized canal engineering; engineer Jozef Kosacki, who Designed to enlarge the existing 100-year-old canal, this $5.25 billion dollar project has redefined world trade routes. By excavating 150 million cubic tons of earth, and by pouring over 4 million cubic meters of concrete, engineers have created two brand-new gigantic flights of locks. Each lock is the length of four football fields, and is controlled by 1650,000 ton steel gates, which enables an unparalleled lift of 26 meters above sea level. The canal is now capable of accommodating the biggest ships on the world's oceans.\\r\\n\\r\\nNone of this would be possible without the work of history's greatest innovators. out what it took to build the largest ship in the world, the Pioneering Spirit. This 900,000-ton behemoth can install oil pipelines in the world's deepest waters and features state-of-the art thrusters and mammoth lifting beams.&quot;,&quot;detailed&quot;:&quot;The Pioneering Spirit is a behemoth of the shipping world. Weighing over 900,000 tons at maximum draft, at 124 meters wide and up to 477 meters long with equipment deployed, this steel giant is the biggest vessel on the planet. Propelled by 12,6000 KW azimuth thrusters, this multi-purpose ship can install and remove oil platforms and lay pipeline in the world's deepest waters. The ship's primary focus is the removal of large steel jacket-based platforms. Its unique dual bow design, with eight pairs of lifting beams, each weighing 1800 tons, enables the ship to straddle a platform, and pick up a 48,000 ton topside, in one Herculean lift.\\r\\nThe innovations on this mega-ship has been inspired by some engineering greats. \\r\\n\\r\\nThis show will feature the work of Alvin Lombard, whose breakthrough continuous tracked logging machine, created Designed to enlarge the existing 100-year-old canal, this $5.25 billion dollar project has redefined world trade routes. By excavating 150 million cubic tons of earth, and by pouring over 4 million cubic meters of concrete, engineers have created two brand-new gigantic flights of locks. Each lock is the length of four football fields, and is controlled by 1650,000 ton steel gates, which enables an unparalleled lift of 26 meters above sea level. The canal is now capable of accommodating the biggest ships on the world's oceans.\\r\\n\\r\\nNone of this would be possible without the work of history's greatest innovators. THE SEARCH is an all-new series featuring the next generation of fearless contenders with killer build skills, science smarts and nerves of steel, ready to be judged each week as they bust myths and vie for the win in becoming the next myth-busting superstars.<\\/p>\\n<p>MythBusters premiered on Discovery Channel in 2003 and would go on to earn eight consecutive Emmy nominations for Outstanding Reality Program from 2009 to 2016. MythBusters fused scientific method with gleeful curiosity and plain old-fashioned ingenuity to create a signature style of explosive experimentation.<\\/p>\\n<p>The series ended in March 2016 after 2,950 experiments, 910 explosions and 83 miles of duct tape. There is a love of busting myths and those with the unflappable curiosity to try it. MYTHBUSTERS: THE SEARCH aims to find these people. <\\/p>\\n<p>Hosted by Kyle Hill - a MythBusters superfan -- MYTHBUSTERS: THE SEARCH marks the start of a new myth-busting era on Science Channel. As host, Hill introduces the contestants and the myths they attempt to bust each week. Using never-before-seen spectacular stunts, some myth-busting challenges will focus on build skills, while others require science know-how; some will test ingenuity, while others will test resolve, all with the goal of busting new myths.<\\/p>\\n<p>In other words, it's the continuing busting of myths, celebration of curiosity, questioning, and experimentation that was the hallmark of the original series -- plus, of course, explosions. <\\/p>\\n<p>Stay tuned; MYTHBUSTERS: THE SEARCH will premiere on Science Channel in THE SEARCH is an all-new series featuring the next generation of fearless contenders with killer build skills, science smarts and nerves of steel, ready to be judged each week as they bust myths and vie for the win in becoming the next myth-busting superstars.<\\/p>\\n<p>MythBusters premiered on Discovery Channel in 2003 and would go on to earn eight consecutive Emmy nominations for Outstanding Reality Program from 2009 to 2016. MythBusters fused scientific method with gleeful curiosity and plain old-fashioned ingenuity to create a signature style of explosive experimentation.<\\/p>\\n<p>The series ended in March 2016 after 2,950 experiments, 910 explosions and 83 miles of duct tape. There is a love of busting myths and those with the unflappable curiosity to try it. MYTHBUSTERS: THE SEARCH aims to find these people. <\\/p>\\n<p>Hosted by Kyle Hill - a MythBusters superfan -- MYTHBUSTERS: THE SEARCH marks the start of a new myth-busting era on Science Channel. As host, Hill introduces the contestants and the myths they attempt to bust each week. Using never-before-seen spectacular stunts, some myth-busting challenges will focus on build skills, while others require science know-how; some will test ingenuity, while others will test resolve, all with the goal of busting new myths.<\\/p>\\n<p>In other words, it's the continuing busting of myths, celebration of curiosity, questioning, and experimentation that was the hallmark of the original series -- plus, of course, explosions. <\\/p>\\n<p>Stay tuned; MYTHBUSTERS: THE SEARCH will premiere on Science Channel in
